export const createSurveyResponseWebhookHeaders = (
  webhook: Webhook,
  body: string,
  messageId: string,
  webhookTimestamp: number
): Record<string, string> => {
  const requestHeaders: Record<string, string> = {
    "content-type": "application/json",
    "webhook-id": messageId,
    "webhook-timestamp": webhookTimestamp.toString(),
  };

  if (webhook.secret) {
    requestHeaders["webhook-signature"] = generateStandardWebhookSignature(
      messageId,
      webhookTimestamp,
      body,
      webhook.secret
    );
  }

  return requestHeaders;
};

const fetchWithTimeout = async (
  url: string,
  options: RequestInit,
  fetchFn: typeof fetch,
  timeoutMs = WEBHOOK_DELIVERY_TIMEOUT_MS
): Promise<Response> => {
  const controller = new AbortController();
  const timeout = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), timeoutMs);

  try {
    return await fetchFn(url, {
      ...options,
      redirect: DANGEROUSLY_ALLOW_WEBHOOK_INTERNAL_URLS ? "follow" : "manual",
      signal: controller.signal,
    });
  } catch (error) {
    if (error instanceof Error && error.name === "AbortError") {
      throw new Error(`Webhook delivery timed out after ${timeoutMs}ms`);
    }
    throw error;
  } finally {
    clearTimeout(timeout);
  }
};

const ensureWebhookSigningSecret = async (webhook: Webhook): Promise<Webhook> => {
  if (webhook.secret) {
    return webhook;
  }

  const secret = generateWebhookSecret();
  const updatedWebhook = await getPrismaWebhookDelegate().update({
    where: { id: webhook.id },
    data: { secret },
  });

  return {
    ...webhook,
    secret: updatedWebhook.secret ?? secret,
  };
};

const getOrCreateWebhookDelivery = async ({
  webhook,
  event,
  environmentId,
  surveyId,
  response,
  payload,
  payloadHash,
  eventKey,
  createMessageId,
}: {
  webhook: Webhook;
  event: PipelineTriggers;
  environmentId: string;
  surveyId: string;
  response: TResponse;
  payload: unknown;
  payloadHash: string;
  eventKey: string;
  createMessageId: () => string;
}): Promise<{ delivery: TWebhookDeliveryRecord; created: boolean }> => {
  const delegate = getWebhookDeliveryDelegate();
  const existingDelivery = await delegate.findUnique({ where: { eventKey } });

  if (existingDelivery) {
    return { delivery: existingDelivery, created: false };
  }

  try {
    const delivery = await delegate.create({
      data: {
        webhookId: webhook.id,
        environmentId,
        surveyId,
        responseId: response.id,
        event,
        eventKey,
        messageId: createMessageId(),
        status: WEBHOOK_DELIVERY_STATUS.PENDING,
        maxAttempts: WEBHOOK_DELIVERY_MAX_ATTEMPTS,
        payload,
        payloadHash,
      },
    });

    return { delivery, created: true };
  } catch (error) {
    if (!isUniqueConstraintError(error)) {
      throw error;
    }

    const racedDelivery = await delegate.findUnique({ where: { eventKey } });
    if (!racedDelivery) {
      throw error;
    }

    return { delivery: racedDelivery, created: false };
  }
};

const recordWebhookDeliveryAttempt = async ({
  delivery,
  attemptNumber,
  status,
  statusCode,
  errorMessage,
  nextRetryAt,
  attemptedAt,
  webhookTimestamp,
}: {
  delivery: TWebhookDeliveryRecord;
  attemptNumber: number;
  status: TWebhookDeliveryStatus;
  statusCode?: number | null;
  errorMessage?: string | null;
  nextRetryAt?: Date | null;
  attemptedAt: Date;
  webhookTimestamp: number | null;
}): Promise<TWebhookDeliveryRecord> => {
  return await getWebhookDeliveryDelegate().update({
    where: { id: delivery.id },
    data: {
      status,
      attemptCount: attemptNumber,
      nextRetryAt: nextRetryAt ?? null,
      lastAttemptAt: attemptedAt,
      deliveredAt: status === WEBHOOK_DELIVERY_STATUS.DELIVERED ? attemptedAt : delivery.deliveredAt,
      lastStatusCode: statusCode ?? null,
      lastError: truncate(errorMessage),
      lastWebhookTimestamp: webhookTimestamp,
    },
  });
};

const recordDeliveryFailure = async ({
  delivery,
  attemptNumber,
  retryable,
  statusCode,
  errorMessage,
  attemptedAt,
  webhookTimestamp,
}: {
  delivery: TWebhookDeliveryRecord;
  attemptNumber: number;
  retryable: boolean;
  statusCode?: number | null;
  errorMessage: string;
  attemptedAt: Date;
  webhookTimestamp: number | null;
}): Promise<DeliveryResult> => {
  const nextRetryAt = retryable ? getNextRetryAt(attemptNumber, delivery.maxAttempts, attemptedAt) : null;
  const status = retryable
    ? nextRetryAt
      ? WEBHOOK_DELIVERY_STATUS.RETRY_SCHEDULED
      : WEBHOOK_DELIVERY_STATUS.EXHAUSTED
    : WEBHOOK_DELIVERY_STATUS.FAILED;

  const updatedDelivery = await recordWebhookDeliveryAttempt({
    delivery,
    attemptNumber,
    status,
    statusCode,
    errorMessage,
    nextRetryAt,
    attemptedAt,
    webhookTimestamp,
  });

  return {
    ok: false,
    status:
      status === WEBHOOK_DELIVERY_STATUS.RETRY_SCHEDULED
        ? "retry_scheduled"
        : status === WEBHOOK_DELIVERY_STATUS.EXHAUSTED
          ? "exhausted"
          : "failed",
    delivery: updatedDelivery,
  };
};

export const attemptWebhookDelivery = async ({
  webhook,
  delivery,
  body,
  requestUrl,
  deps,
}: AttemptWebhookDeliveryInput): Promise<DeliveryResult> => {
  const now = deps?.now ?? (() => new Date());
  const fetchFn = deps?.fetchFn ?? fetch;
  const attemptNumber = delivery.attemptCount + 1;
  const attemptedAt = now();
  let webhookTimestamp: number | null = null;

  try {
    const signedWebhook = await ensureWebhookSigningSecret(webhook);
    await validateWebhookUrl(signedWebhook.url);

    webhookTimestamp = Math.floor(attemptedAt.getTime() / 1000);
    const headers = createSurveyResponseWebhookHeaders(
      signedWebhook,
      body,
      delivery.messageId,
      webhookTimestamp
    );

    const fetchResponse = await fetchWithTimeout(
      signedWebhook.url,
      {
        method: "POST",
        headers,
        body,
      },
      fetchFn
    );

    if (fetchResponse.status >= 200 && fetchResponse.status < 300) {
      const updatedDelivery = await recordWebhookDeliveryAttempt({
        delivery,
        attemptNumber,
        status: WEBHOOK_DELIVERY_STATUS.DELIVERED,
        statusCode: fetchResponse.status,
        attemptedAt,
        webhookTimestamp,
      });

      return { ok: true, status: "delivered", delivery: updatedDelivery };
    }

    const redirectBlocked =
      !DANGEROUSLY_ALLOW_WEBHOOK_INTERNAL_URLS && fetchResponse.status >= 300 && fetchResponse.status < 400;
    const errorMessage = redirectBlocked
      ? "Webhook endpoint returned a redirect, which is not allowed"
      : `Webhook endpoint returned HTTP ${fetchResponse.status}`;

    return await recordDeliveryFailure({
      delivery,
      attemptNumber,
      retryable: !redirectBlocked && isRetryableStatusCode(fetchResponse.status),
      statusCode: fetchResponse.status,
      errorMessage,
      attemptedAt,
      webhookTimestamp,
    });
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error(
      { error, webhookId: webhook.id, deliveryId: delivery.id, url: requestUrl },
      "Webhook delivery failed"
    );

    return await recordDeliveryFailure({
      delivery,
      attemptNumber,
      retryable: !isInvalidWebhookUrlError(error),
      errorMessage: toErrorMessage(error),
      attemptedAt,
      webhookTimestamp,
    });
  }
};

  webhook,
  event,
  response,
  survey,
  responseData,
  environmentId,
  surveyId,
  requestUrl,
  deps,
}: DeliverSurveyResponseWebhookInput): Promise<DeliveryResult> => {
  const payload = buildSurveyResponseWebhookPayload({ webhook, event, response, survey, responseData });
  const body = serializePayload(payload);
```

export const processDueWebhookDeliveries = async ({
  limit = 50,
  requestUrl,
  deps,
}: {
  limit?: number;
  requestUrl?: string;
  deps?: Omit<WebhookDeliveryDeps, "createMessageId">;
} = {}): Promise<{ processed: number; results: DeliveryResult[] }> => {
  const now = deps?.now ?? (() => new Date());
  const dueAt = now();
  const delegate = getWebhookDeliveryDelegate();
  const dueDeliveries = (await delegate.findMany({
    where: {
      status: WEBHOOK_DELIVERY_STATUS.RETRY_SCHEDULED,
      nextRetryAt: {
        lte: dueAt,
      },
    },
    include: {
      webhook: true,
    },
    orderBy: [{ nextRetryAt: "asc" }, { createdAt: "asc" }],
    take: limit,
  })) as Array<TWebhookDeliveryRecord & { webhook?: Webhook | null }>;

  const results: DeliveryResult[] = [];

  for (const delivery of dueDeliveries) {
    const claimed = await delegate.updateMany({
      where: {
        id: delivery.id,
        status: WEBHOOK_DELIVERY_STATUS.RETRY_SCHEDULED,
        nextRetryAt: {
          lte: dueAt,
        },
      },
      data: {
        status: WEBHOOK_DELIVERY_STATUS.PENDING,
        nextRetryAt: null,
      },
    });

    if (claimed.count !== 1) {
      results.push({ ok: true, status: "skipped", delivery });
      continue;
    }

    if (!delivery.webhook) {
      const failedDelivery = await recordWebhookDeliveryAttempt({
        delivery,
        attemptNumber: delivery.attemptCount,
        status: WEBHOOK_DELIVERY_STATUS.FAILED,
        errorMessage: "Webhook endpoint no longer exists",
        attemptedAt: dueAt,
        webhookTimestamp: null,
      });
      results.push({ ok: false, status: "failed", delivery: failedDelivery });
      continue;
    }

    results.push(
      await attemptWebhookDelivery({
        webhook: delivery.webhook,
        delivery: {
          ...delivery,
          status: WEBHOOK_DELIVERY_STATUS.PENDING,
          nextRetryAt: null,
        },
        body: serializePayload(delivery.payload),
        requestUrl,
        deps,
      })
    );
  }

  return {
    processed: results.length,
    results,
  };
};

export const getWebhookDeliveryLogs = async ({
  webhookId,
  limit = 50,
  skip = 0,
  status,
  event,
  responseId,
  sortBy = "createdAt",
  order = "desc",
}: { webhookId: string } & DeliveryLogFilter): Promise<{
  data: TWebhookDeliveryLog[];
  total: number;
  limit: number;
  offset: number;
}> => {
  const delegate = getWebhookDeliveryDelegate();
  const where = {
    webhookId,
    ...(status && { status }),
    ...(event && { event }),
    ...(responseId && { responseId }),
  };
  const [deliveries, total] = await Promise.all([
    delegate.findMany({
      where,
      select: {
        id: true,
        createdAt: true,
        updatedAt: true,
        webhookId: true,
        environmentId: true,
        surveyId: true,
        responseId: true,
        event: true,
        messageId: true,
        status: true,
        attemptCount: true,
        maxAttempts: true,
        nextRetryAt: true,
        lastAttemptAt: true,
        deliveredAt: true,
        lastStatusCode: true,
        lastError: true,
        lastWebhookTimestamp: true,
        payloadHash: true,
      },
      orderBy: [{ [sortBy]: order }, { id: "desc" }],
      take: limit,
      skip,
    }),
    delegate.count({ where }),
  ]);

  return {
    data: deliveries as TWebhookDeliveryLog[],
    total,
    limit,
    offset: skip,
  };
};
```
